aria-haspopup="true">Shared publicly</span> &nbsp;-&nbsp; <span class="uv PL"><a href="109625418534467664286/posts/VAbgBbB2GvC" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="o-U-s FI Rg" style="display:none" >2014-10-24</a></span></span></header></div><div class="QM"><div class="zda Zg"><div class="gn Br Hh kv" data-topicindex="1"><span class="Hh Nu">&nbsp;</span><a href="explore/RAW" target="_top" class="d-s ob MK Dd" aria-label="#RAW" tabindex="0" jsaction="click:TWICud" jsname="WpESUd" data-topicid="/hashtag/raw">#RAW</a></div><div class="gn Br Hh Zk" data-topicindex="2"><span class="Hh Ou">&nbsp;</span><a href="explore/Lightroom" target="_top" class="d-s ob MK Dd" aria-label="#Lightroom" tabindex="0" jsaction="click:TWICud" jsname="WpESUd" data-topicid="/hashtag/lightroom">#Lightroom</a></div></div></div></div><div class="Al pf"><div class="Xx xJ"><div class="Ig At dn"><div class=""><div class="tG QF">&nbsp;</div><div class="Ct">I&#39;ve been looking forward to see reviews since I finished implementing the RAW DNG profiling and calibration for <span class="proflinkWrapper"><span class="proflinkPrefix">+</span><a class="proflink aaTEdf" href="/115576844812998187455" oid="115576844812998187455">Cyanogen Inc.</a></span> on the OnePlus One a couple months ago.<br><br><span class="proflinkWrapper"><span class="proflinkPrefix">+</span><a class="proflink aaTEdf" href="/101627796727750366106" oid="101627796727750366106">Tek Syndicate</a></span> just published one in video and they&#39;re pretty enthusiasts about the results :)<br><br>A tip about converter software: <span class="proflinkWrapper"><span class="proflinkPrefix">+</span><a class="proflink aaTEdf" href="/115446348255335388307" oid="115446348255335388307">Albert Manduca</a></span>, who shows his experience with RAW editing  uses <span class="proflinkWrapper"><span class="proflinkPrefix">+</span><a class="proflink aaTEdf" href="/115209321914160323553" oid="115209321914160323553">Adobe</a></span> Lightroom which is great as it&#39;s one of the software that implement all the DNG capabilities I used during profiling.<br>Mainly:<br>* Color calibration<br>* Noise profiling<br>* Lens vignetting correction and sensor color uniformity<br><br>DNG files are the RAW sensor data plus metadata that describe shooting conditions and how to transform what the sensor sees into a corrected image representing colors as they are.<br>Compared to proprietary RAW formats, DNG is self-describing.<br><br>Smartphones&#39; captures require more correction than other cameras due to their physical constrains.<br>Some converters support DNG but not all its features.<br>Typically, noise, vignette or color uniformity won&#39;t be corrected as expected, color conversion incomplete, exposure compensation not applied so be sure to use a fully fledged RAW editor!<br><br>By the way, did anyone made a comparison with a Lumia DNG?﻿</div></div></div></div><div class="yx Nf"><div itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/VideoObject" class="j9"><div class="q9 yg"><div class="sp ej bc ,"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-z_-AAEJOqCA/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAArnE/a3YD12Be1W8/photo.jpg",,"I've been looking forward to see reviews since I finished implementing the RAW DNG profiling and calibration for +Cyanogen Inc. on the OnePlus One a couple months ago.\n\n+Tek Syndicate just published one in video and they're pretty enthusiasts about the results :)\n\nA tip about converter software: +Albert Manduca, who shows his experience with RAW editing  uses +Adobe Lightroom which is great as it's one of the software that implement all the DNG capabilities I used during profiling.\nMainly:\n* Color calibration\n* Noise profiling\n* Lens vignetting correction and sensor color uniformity\n\nDNG files are the RAW sensor data plus metadata that describe shooting conditions and how to transform what the sensor sees into a corrected image representing colors as they are.\nCompared to proprietary RAW formats, DNG is self-describing.\n\nSmartphones' captures require more correction than other cameras due to their physical constrains.\nSome converters support DNG but not all its features.\nTypically, noise, vignette or color uniformity won't be corrected as expected, color conversion incomplete, exposure compensation not applied so be sure to use a fully fledged RAW editor!\n\nBy the way, did anyone made a comparison with a Lumia
